                       LGBTQ friendly. I have a dog! This AirBnB is for a simple, tiny guest bedroom. The room has a dresser for you to place your clothes/belongings in. It used to double as my office so I have a filing cabinet and printer there for now. No real amenities. The room is clean and bright. The twin bed has large drawers for you to store things as well. There is a bookshelf with random reading material if you choose to read some as well. Depending on when you stay, you will share the bathroom with me. Some nights, I won't be home. I will be staying in the bedroom down the hall. * I have two other housemates on the other end of the house. They have their own bathroom and own schedules. BOOKING YOUR STAY - It is expected that guests have personal or professional business in the area. After you read my entire listing and complete your profile with photo and verification, please send me a description of your travel plans and expected arrival time and I will quickly respond to your inquiry.                       <div data-reactid="2262">
                       Private Room with lock in Mid-City area of Los Angeles. Shared bathroom. Wifi.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="2263">
                       The room has a Queen-size bed. We provide bed-sheets. This is a boardinghouse/hostel, with several private rooms that are all rented out. Each room has a lock.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="2264">
                       Great Central Location in Los Angeles, near the intersection of La Brea Ave and Venice Blvd. La Brea Ave is one of the streets that everybody in Los Angeles knows. Going North, it will take you straight to the heart of Hollywood, the hand/footprints of the stars at the Chinese Theatre, Dolby Theatre, Hollywood Wax Museum, Guinnes World of Records Museum, Hollywood Museum, as well as numerous shops and restaurants along the Hollywood Walk of Fame. Going south on La Brea is a great way to get to LAX airport to avoid freeway traffic.
                      </div>
